namespace = cpbm_independence_europe

##########################
###MODERN NATION STATES###
##########################

#Iceland
country_event = {
	id = cpbm_independence_europe.1
	title = cpbm_independence_europe.1.t
	desc = cpbm_independence_europe.1.d
	picture = MILITARY_CAMP_eventPicture

	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	option = {
		name = cpbm_independence_europe.1.a
		add_adm_power = -200
		add_dip_power = -200
		add_mil_power = -200
		every_owned_province = { 
			limit = { area = iceland_area }
			cede_province = ICE
			add_core = ICE
			remove_core = ROOT 
		}
		vassalize = ICE
		ICE = { set_capital = 370 }
	}
	
	option = {
		name = cpbm_independence_europe.1.b
		every_owned_province = { 
			limit = { area = iceland_area }
			cede_province = ICE
			add_core = ICE
			remove_core = ROOT 
		}
		ICE = { 
			every_neighbor_country = { add_truce_with = ICE } 
			set_capital = 370
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = cpbm_independence_europe.1.c
		trigger = { AND = { adm_power = 100 dip_power = 100 mil_power = 100 } }
		add_adm_power = -200
		add_dip_power = -200
		add_mil_power = -200
		add_years_of_income = -2
		every_owned_province = { 
			limit = { area = iceland_area }
			add_unrest = 5
			add_core = ICE
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = cpbm_independence_europe.1.dd
		every_owned_province = { 
			limit = { area = iceland_area }
			cede_province = ICE
			add_core = ICE
		}
		ICE = { 
			declare_war_with_cb = {
				who = ROOT
				casus_belli = cb_independence_war
			}
			set_capital = 370
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			ICE = {
				capital_scope = {
					build_to_forcelimit = {
						infantry = 0.8
						cavalry = 0.2
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}
    
    after = { 370 = { every_core_country = { limit = { tag = ICE } change_primary_culture = PREV change_religion = PREV change_government = ROOT } }
		ICE = { every_province = { limit = { owned_by = ROOT is_in_capital_area = no NOT = { range = ROOT } trade_range = PREV } cede_province = PREV add_core = PREV }
		every_owned_province = { limit = { is_in_capital_area = no NOT = { range = PREV } trade_range = ROOT } cede_province = ROOT add_core = ROOT } }
		random_list = { 1 = { country_event = { id = cpbm_independence_trigger.1 } } 9 = { } }
	}
}

#Finland
country_event = {
	id = cpbm_independence_europe.2
	title = cpbm_independence_europe.2.t
	desc = cpbm_independence_europe.2.d
	picture = MILITARY_CAMP_eventPicture

	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	option = {
		name = cpbm_independence_europe.2.a
		add_adm_power = -200
		add_dip_power = -200
		add_mil_power = -200
		every_owned_province = { 
			limit = {
				OR = { 
                    area = finland_area
                    area = bothnia_area
					province_id = 1930
					province_id = 4152
				}
			}
			cede_province = FIN
			add_core = FIN
			remove_core = ROOT 
		}
		vassalize = FIN
		FIN = { set_capital = 28 }
	}
	
	option = {
		name = cpbm_independence_europe.2.b
		every_owned_province = { 
			limit = {
				OR = { 
                    area = finland_area
                    area = bothnia_area
					province_id = 1930
					province_id = 4152
				}
			}
			cede_province = FIN
			add_core = FIN
			remove_core = ROOT 
		}
		FIN = { 
			every_neighbor_country = { add_truce_with = FIN } 
			set_capital = 28
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = cpbm_independence_europe.2.c
		trigger = { AND = { adm_power = 100 dip_power = 100 mil_power = 100 } }
		add_adm_power = -200
		add_dip_power = -200
		add_mil_power = -200
		add_years_of_income = -2
		every_owned_province = { 
			limit = {
				OR = { 
                    area = finland_area
                    area = bothnia_area
					province_id = 1930
					province_id = 4152
				}
			}
			add_unrest = 5
			add_core = FIN
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = cpbm_independence_europe.2.dd
		every_owned_province = { 
			limit = {
				OR = { 
                    area = finland_area
                    area = bothnia_area
					province_id = 1930
					province_id = 4152
				}
			}
			cede_province = FIN
			add_core = FIN
		}
		FIN = { 
			declare_war_with_cb = {
				who = ROOT
				casus_belli = cb_independence_war
			}
			set_capital = 28
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			FIN = {
				capital_scope = {
					build_to_forcelimit = {
						infantry = 0.8
						cavalry = 0.2
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}
    
    after = { 28 = { every_core_country = { limit = { tag = FIN } change_primary_culture = PREV change_religion = PREV change_government = ROOT } }
		FIN = { every_province = { limit = { owned_by = ROOT is_in_capital_area = no NOT = { range = ROOT } trade_range = PREV } cede_province = PREV add_core = PREV }
		every_owned_province = { limit = { is_in_capital_area = no NOT = { range = PREV } trade_range = ROOT } cede_province = ROOT add_core = ROOT } }
		random_list = { 1 = { country_event = { id = cpbm_independence_trigger.1 } } 9 = { } }
	}
}

#Norway
country_event = {
	id = cpbm_independence_europe.3
	title = cpbm_independence_europe.3.t
	desc = cpbm_independence_europe.3.d
	picture = MILITARY_CAMP_eventPicture

	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	option = {
		name = cpbm_independence_europe.3.a
		add_adm_power = -200
		add_dip_power = -200
		add_mil_power = -200
		every_owned_province = { 
			limit = {
				OR = { 
                    area = eastern_norway
                    area = western_norway
                    area = northern_norway
                    area = subarctic_islands_area
                    area = iceland_area
					province_id = 5
					province_id = 8
					province_id = 16
					province_id = 315
					province_id = 4164
				}
			}
			cede_province = NOR
			add_core = NOR
			remove_core = ROOT 
		}
		vassalize = NOR
		NOR = { set_capital = 17 }
	}
	
	option = {
		name = cpbm_independence_europe.3.b
		every_owned_province = { 
			limit = {
				OR = { 
                    area = eastern_norway
                    area = western_norway
                    area = northern_norway
                    area = subarctic_islands_area
                    area = iceland_area
					province_id = 5
					province_id = 8
					province_id = 16
					province_id = 315
					province_id = 4164
				}
			}
			cede_province = NOR
			add_core = NOR
			remove_core = ROOT 
		}
		NOR = { 
			every_neighbor_country = { add_truce_with = NOR } 
			set_capital = 17
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = cpbm_independence_europe.3.c
		trigger = { AND = { adm_power = 100 dip_power = 100 mil_power = 100 } }
		add_adm_power = -200
		add_dip_power = -200
		add_mil_power = -200
		add_years_of_income = -2
		every_owned_province = { 
			limit = {
				OR = { 
                    area = eastern_norway
                    area = western_norway
                    area = northern_norway
                    area = subarctic_islands_area
                    area = iceland_area
					province_id = 5
					province_id = 8
					province_id = 16
					province_id = 315
					province_id = 4164
				}
			}
			add_unrest = 5
			add_core = NOR
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = cpbm_independence_europe.3.dd
		every_owned_province = { 
			limit = {
				OR = { 
                    area = eastern_norway
                    area = western_norway
                    area = northern_norway
                    area = subarctic_islands_area
                    area = iceland_area
					province_id = 5
					province_id = 8
					province_id = 16
					province_id = 315
					province_id = 4164
				}
			}
			cede_province = NOR
			add_core = NOR
		}
		NOR = { 
			declare_war_with_cb = {
				who = ROOT
				casus_belli = cb_independence_war
			}
			set_capital = 17
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			NOR = {
				capital_scope = {
					build_to_forcelimit = {
						infantry = 0.8
						cavalry = 0.2
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}
    
    after = { 17 = { every_core_country = { limit = { tag = NOR } change_primary_culture = PREV change_religion = PREV change_government = ROOT } }
		NOR = { every_province = { limit = { owned_by = ROOT is_in_capital_area = no NOT = { range = ROOT } trade_range = PREV } cede_province = PREV add_core = PREV }
		every_owned_province = { limit = { is_in_capital_area = no NOT = { range = PREV } trade_range = ROOT } cede_province = ROOT add_core = ROOT } }
		random_list = { 1 = { country_event = { id = cpbm_independence_trigger.1 } } 9 = { } }
	}
}

#Sweden
country_event = {
	id = cpbm_independence_europe.4
	title = cpbm_independence_europe.4.t
	desc = cpbm_independence_europe.4.d
	picture = MILITARY_CAMP_eventPicture

	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	option = {
		name = cpbm_independence_europe.4.a
		add_adm_power = -200
		add_dip_power = -200
		add_mil_power = -200
		every_owned_province = { 
			limit = {
				OR = { 
                    area = ostra_svealand_area
                    area = norrland_area
                    area = svealand_area
                    area = gotaland_area
                    area = finland_area
                    area = bothnia_area
                    area = eastern_norway
                    area = western_norway
                    area = northern_norway
                    area = vastra_gotaland_area
                    area = skaneland_area
                    area = eastern_norway
                    area = western_norway
                    area = northern_norway
                    area = subarctic_islands_area
                    area = iceland_area
					province_id = 315
					province_id = 1981
					province_id = 4152
				}
			}
			cede_province = SWE
			add_core = SWE
			remove_core = ROOT 
		}
		vassalize = SWE
		SWE = { set_capital = 1 }
	}
	
	option = {
		name = cpbm_independence_europe.4.b
		every_owned_province = { 
			limit = {
				OR = { 
                    area = ostra_svealand_area
                    area = norrland_area
                    area = svealand_area
                    area = gotaland_area
                    area = finland_area
                    area = bothnia_area
                    area = eastern_norway
                    area = western_norway
                    area = northern_norway
                    area = vastra_gotaland_area
                    area = skaneland_area
                    area = eastern_norway
                    area = western_norway
                    area = northern_norway
                    area = subarctic_islands_area
                    area = iceland_area
					province_id = 315
					province_id = 1981
					province_id = 4152
				}
			}
			cede_province = SWE
			add_core = SWE
			remove_core = ROOT 
		}
		SWE = { 
			every_neighbor_country = { add_truce_with = SWE } 
			set_capital = 1
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = cpbm_independence_europe.4.c
		trigger = { AND = { adm_power = 100 dip_power = 100 mil_power = 100 } }
		add_adm_power = -200
		add_dip_power = -200
		add_mil_power = -200
		add_years_of_income = -2
		every_owned_province = { 
			limit = {
				OR = { 
                    area = ostra_svealand_area
                    area = norrland_area
                    area = svealand_area
                    area = gotaland_area
                    area = finland_area
                    area = bothnia_area
                    area = eastern_norway
                    area = western_norway
                    area = northern_norway
                    area = vastra_gotaland_area
                    area = skaneland_area
                    area = eastern_norway
                    area = western_norway
                    area = northern_norway
                    area = subarctic_islands_area
                    area = iceland_area
					province_id = 315
					province_id = 1981
					province_id = 4152
				}
			}
			add_unrest = 5
			add_core = SWE
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = cpbm_independence_europe.4.dd
		every_owned_province = { 
			limit = {
				OR = { 
                    area = ostra_svealand_area
                    area = norrland_area
                    area = svealand_area
                    area = gotaland_area
                    area = finland_area
                    area = bothnia_area
                    area = eastern_norway
                    area = western_norway
                    area = northern_norway
                    area = vastra_gotaland_area
                    area = skaneland_area
                    area = eastern_norway
                    area = western_norway
                    area = northern_norway
                    area = subarctic_islands_area
                    area = iceland_area
					province_id = 315
					province_id = 1981
					province_id = 4152
				}
			}
			cede_province = SWE
			add_core = SWE
		}
		SWE = { 
			declare_war_with_cb = {
				who = ROOT
				casus_belli = cb_independence_war
			}
			set_capital = 1
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			SWE = {
				capital_scope = {
					build_to_forcelimit = {
						infantry = 0.8
						cavalry = 0.2
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}
    
    after = { 1 = { every_core_country = { limit = { tag = SWE } change_primary_culture = PREV change_religion = PREV change_government = ROOT } }
		SWE = { every_province = { limit = { owned_by = ROOT is_in_capital_area = no NOT = { range = ROOT } trade_range = PREV } cede_province = PREV add_core = PREV }
		every_owned_province = { limit = { is_in_capital_area = no NOT = { range = PREV } trade_range = ROOT } cede_province = ROOT add_core = ROOT } }
		random_list = { 1 = { country_event = { id = cpbm_independence_trigger.1 } } 9 = { } }
	}
}

#Denmark
country_event = {
	id = cpbm_independence_europe.5
	title = cpbm_independence_europe.5.t
	desc = cpbm_independence_europe.5.d
	picture = MILITARY_CAMP_eventPicture

	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	option = {
		name = cpbm_independence_europe.5.a
		add_adm_power = -200
		add_dip_power = -200
		add_mil_power = -200
		every_owned_province = { 
			limit = {
				OR = { 
                    area = denmark_area
                    area = jutland_area
                    area = skaneland_area
                    area = eastern_norway
                    area = western_norway
                    area = northern_norway
                    area = iceland_area
					province_id = 3
					province_id = 16
					province_id = 25
					province_id = 315
					province_id = 1979
					province_id = 4166
				}
			}
			cede_province = DAN
			add_core = DAN
			remove_core = ROOT 
		}
		vassalize = DAN
		DAN = { set_capital = 12 }
	}
	
	option = {
		name = cpbm_independence_europe.5.b
		every_owned_province = {

				}
			}
			add_unrest = 5
			add_core = DAN
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = cpbm_independence_europe.5.dd

				OR = { 
                    area = denmark_area

					province_id = 1979
					province_id = 4166

#Netherlands

	id = cpbm_independence_europe.6
	title = cpbm_independence_europe.6.t
	desc = cpbm_independence_europe.6.d

			limit = {
				OR = { 
                    area = holland_area
                    area = frisia_area
                    area = north_brabant_area
                    area = brabant_area
					province_id = 90
					province_id = 91
					province_id = 93
					province_id = 1865
					province_id = 1866
				}
			}

#Belgium
country_event = {
	id = cpbm_independence_europe.7
	title = cpbm_independence_europe.7.t
	desc = cpbm_independence_europe.7.d
	picture = MILITARY_CAMP_eventPicture

	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	option = {
		name = cpbm_independence_europe.7.a
		add_adm_power = -200
		add_dip_power = -200
		add_mil_power = -200
		every_owned_province = { 
			limit = {
				OR = { 
                    area = brabant_area
					province_id = 90
					province_id = 91
					province_id = 93
					province_id = 1865
					province_id = 1866
					province_id = 3004
				}
			}
			cede_province = BEL
			add_core = BEL
			remove_core = ROOT 
		}
		vassalize = BEL
		BEL = { set_capital = 92 }
	}
	
	option = {
		name = cpbm_independence_europe.7.b
		every_owned_province = { 
			limit = {
				OR = { 
                    area = brabant_area
					province_id = 90
					province_id = 91
					province_id = 93
					province_id = 1865
					province_id = 1866
					province_id = 3004
				}
			}
			cede_province = BEL
			add_core = BEL
			remove_core = ROOT 
		}
		BEL = { 
			every_neighbor_country = { add_truce_with = BEL } 
			set_capital = 92
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = cpbm_independence_europe.7.c
		trigger = { AND = { adm_power = 100 dip_power = 100 mil_power = 100 } }
		add_adm_power = -200
		add_dip_power = -200
		add_mil_power = -200
		add_years_of_income = -2
		every_owned_province = { 
			limit = {
				OR = { 
                    area = brabant_area
					province_id = 90
					province_id = 91
					province_id = 93
					province_id = 1865
					province_id = 1866
					province_id = 3004
				}
			}
			add_unrest = 5
			add_core = BEL
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = cpbm_independence_europe.7.dd
		every_owned_province = { 
			limit = {
				OR = { 
                    area = brabant_area
					province_id = 90
					province_id = 91
					province_id = 93
					province_id = 1865
					province_id = 1866
					province_id = 3004
				}
			}
			cede_province = BEL
			add_core = BEL
		}
		BEL = { 
			declare_war_with_cb = {
				who = ROOT
				casus_belli = cb_independence_war
			}
			set_capital = 92
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			BEL = {
				capital_scope = {
					build_to_forcelimit = {
						infantry = 0.8
						cavalry = 0.2
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}
    
    after = { 92 = { every_core_country = { limit = { tag = BEL } change_primary_culture = PREV change_religion = PREV change_government = ROOT } }
		BEL = { every_province = { limit = { owned_by = ROOT is_in_capital_area = no NOT = { range = ROOT } trade_range = PREV } cede_province = PREV add_core = PREV }
		every_owned_province = { limit = { is_in_capital_area = no NOT = { range = PREV } trade_range = ROOT } cede_province = ROOT add_core = ROOT } }
		random_list = { 1 = { country_event = { id = cpbm_independence_trigger.1 } } 9 = { } }
	}
}

#Ireland
country_event = {
	id = cpbm_independence_europe.9
	title = cpbm_independence_europe.9.t
	desc = cpbm_independence_europe.9.d
	picture = MILITARY_CAMP_eventPicture

	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	option = {
		name = cpbm_independence_europe.9.a
		add_adm_power = -200
		add_dip_power = -200
		add_mil_power = -200
		every_owned_province = { 
			limit = {
				OR = { 
                    area = munster_area 
                    area = connacht_area
                    area = leinster_area
                    area = ulster_area 
				}
			}
			cede_province = IRE
			add_core = IRE
			remove_core = ROOT 
		}
		vassalize = IRE
		IRE = { set_capital = 373 }
	}
	
	option = {
		name = cpbm_independence_europe.9.b
		every_owned_province = { 
			limit = {
				OR = { 
                    area = munster_area 
                    area = connacht_area
                    area = leinster_area
                    area = ulster_area 
				}
			}
			cede_province = IRE
			add_core = IRE
			remove_core = ROOT 
		}
		IRE = { 
			every_neighbor_country = { add_truce_with = IRE } 
			set_capital = 373
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = cpbm_independence_europe.9.c
		trigger = { AND = { adm_power = 100 dip_power = 100 mil_power = 100 } }
		add_adm_power = -200
		add_dip_power = -200
		add_mil_power = -200
		add_years_of_income = -2
		every_owned_province = { 
			limit = {
				OR = { 
                    area = munster_area 
                    area = connacht_area
                    area = leinster_area
                    area = ulster_area 
				}
			}
			add_unrest = 5
			add_core = IRE
		}
	}
	
	option = {

			limit = {
				OR = { 
                    area = munster_area 
                    area = connacht_area
                    area = leinster_area
                    area = ulster_area 
				}

					}

		}

    after = { 373 = { every_core_country = { limit = { tag = IRE } change_primary_culture = PREV change_religion = PREV change_government = ROOT } }
		IRE = { every_province = { limit = { owned_by = ROOT is_in_capital_area = no NOT = { range = ROOT } trade_range = PREV } cede_province = PREV add_core = PREV }

		add_mil_power = -200
		every_owned_province = { 
			limit = { region = british_isles_region }

			remove_core = ROOT 
		}
		vassalize = GBR

		}

		add_dip_power = -200

                    region = north_german_region
                    region = south_german_region
				}
			}
			cede_province = GER
			add_core = GER
			remove_core = ROOT 
		}
		vassalize = GER
		GER = { set_capital = 50 }
	}
	
	option = {
		name = cpbm_independence_europe.14.b
		every_owned_province = { 
			limit = {
				OR = { 
                    region = north_german_region
                    region = south_german_region
				}
			}
			cede_province = GER
			add_core = GER
			remove_core = ROOT 
		}
		GER = { 
			every_neighbor_country = { add_truce_with = GER } 
			set_capital = 50
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = cpbm_independence_europe.14.c
		trigger = { AND = { adm_power = 100 dip_power = 100 mil_power = 100 } }
		add_adm_power = -200
		add_dip_power = -200
		add_mil_power = -200
		add_years_of_income = -2
		every_owned_province = { 
			limit = {
				OR = { 
                    region = north_german_region
                    region = south_german_region
				}
			}
			add_unrest = 5
			add_core = GER
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = cpbm_independence_europe.14.dd
		every_owned_province = { 
			limit = {
				OR = { 
                    region = north_german_region
                    region = south_german_region
				}
			}
			cede_province = GER
			add_core = GER
		}
		GER = { 
			declare_war_with_cb = {
				who = ROOT
				casus_belli = cb_independence_war
			}
			set_capital = 50
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			GER = {
				capital_scope = {
					build_to_forcelimit = {
						infantry = 0.8
						cavalry = 0.2
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}
    
    after = { 50 = { every_core_country = { limit = { tag = GER } change_primary_culture = PREV change_religion = PREV change_government = ROOT } }
		GER = { every_province = { limit = { owned_by = ROOT is_in_capital_area = no NOT = { range = ROOT } trade_range = PREV } cede_province = PREV add_core = PREV }
		every_owned_province = { limit = { is_in_capital_area = no NOT = { range = PREV } trade_range = ROOT } cede_province = ROOT add_core = ROOT } }
		random_list = { 1 = { country_event = { id = cpbm_independence_trigger.1 } } 9 = { } }
	}
}

#Austria
country_event = {
	id = cpbm_independence_europe.15
	title = cpbm_independence_europe.15.t
	desc = cpbm_independence_europe.15.d
	picture = MILITARY_CAMP_eventPicture

	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	option = {
		name = cpbm_independence_europe.15.a
		add_adm_power = -200
		add_dip_power = -200
		add_mil_power = -200
		every_owned_province = { 
			limit = {
				OR = { 
                    area = austria_proper_area
                    area = inner_austria_area
                    area = east_bavaria_area
                    area = tirol_area
                    area = carinthia_area
                    area = lower_bavaria_area
                    area = upper_bavaria_area
                    area = upper_swabia_area
                    area = lower_swabia_area
					province_id = 72
					province_id = 1880
				}
			}
			cede_province = HAB
			add_core = HAB
			remove_core = ROOT 
		}
		vassalize = HAB
		HAB = { set_capital = 134 }
	}
	
	option = {
		name = cpbm_independence_europe.15.b
		every_owned_province = { 
			limit = {
				OR = { 
                    area = austria_proper_area

                    area = east_bavaria_area
                    area = tirol_area
                    area = carinthia_area
                    area = lower_bavaria_area
                    area = upper_bavaria_area
                    area = upper_swabia_area
                    area = lower_swabia_area
					province_id = 72
					province_id = 1880
				}
			}
			cede_province = HAB
			add_core = HAB
			remove_core = ROOT 
		}
		HAB = { 
			every_neighbor_country = { add_truce_with = HAB } 
			set_capital = 134
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = cpbm_independence_europe.15.c
		trigger = { AND = { adm_power = 100 dip_power = 100 mil_power = 100 } }
		add_adm_power = -200
		add_dip_power = -200
		add_mil_power = -200
		add_years_of_income = -2
		every_owned_province = {

                    area = upper_bavaria_area

                    area = lower_swabia_area
					province_id = 72
					province_id = 1880
				}
			}
			add_unrest = 5
			add_core = HAB
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = cpbm_independence_europe.15.dd
		every_owned_province = { 
			limit = {
				OR = { 
                    area = austria_proper_area
                    area = inner_austria_area
                    area = east_bavaria_area
                    area = tirol_area
                    area = carinthia_area
                    area = lower_bavaria_area
                    area = upper_bavaria_area
                    area = upper_swabia_area
                    area = lower_swabia_area
					province_id = 72
					province_id = 1880
				}
			}
			cede_province = HAB
			add_core = HAB
		}
		HAB = { 
			declare_war_with_cb = {
				who = ROOT
				casus_belli = cb_independence_war
			}
			set_capital = 134
		}

						cavalry = 0.2
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}
    
    after = { 134 = { every_core_country = { limit = { tag = HAB } change_primary_culture = PREV change_religion = PREV change_government = ROOT } }
		HAB = { every_province = { limit = { owned_by = ROOT is_in_capital_area = no NOT = { range = ROOT } trade_range = PREV } cede_province = PREV add_core = PREV }
		every_owned_province = { limit = { is_in_capital_area = no NOT = { range = PREV } trade_range = ROOT } cede_province = ROOT add_core = ROOT } }

		name = cpbm_independence_europe.21.dd
		every_owned_province = { 
			limit = {
				OR = { 
                    area = bohemia_area
                    area = erzgebirge_area
                    area = lusatia_area
                    area = moravia_area
				}
			}
			cede_province = CZE
			add_core = CZE
		}
		CZE = { 
			declare_war_with_cb = {
				who = ROOT
				casus_belli = cb_independence_war
			}
			set_capital = 266
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			CZE = {
				capital_scope = {
					build_to_forcelimit = {
						infantry = 0.8
						cavalry = 0.2
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}
    
    after = { 266 = { every_core_country = { limit = { tag = CZE } change_primary_culture = PREV change_religion = PREV change_government = ROOT } }
		CZE = { every_province = { limit = { owned_by = ROOT is_in_capital_area = no NOT = { range = ROOT } trade_range = PREV } cede_province = PREV add_core = PREV }

	desc = cpbm_independence_europe.22.d
	picture = MILITARY_CAMP_eventPicture

		add_dip_power = -200
		add_mil_power = -200
		every_owned_province = { 
			limit = { area = slovakia_area }
			cede_province = SVK
			add_core = SVK
			remove_core = ROOT 
		}
		vassalize = SVK
		SVK = { set_capital = 1772 }
	}

		name = cpbm_independence_europe.22.b

			limit = { area = slovakia_area }

			add_core = SVK
			remove_core = ROOT 
		}

		}

		add_dip_power = -200
		add_mil_power = -200

#North Macedonia
country_event = {
	id = cpbm_independence_europe.29
	title = cpbm_independence_europe.29.t
	desc = cpbm_independence_europe.29.d
	picture = MILITARY_CAMP_eventPicture

	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	option = {
		name = cpbm_independence_europe.29.a
		add_adm_power = -200
		add_dip_power = -200
		add_mil_power = -200
		every_owned_province = { 
			limit = {
				OR = { 
					province_id = 3001
					province_id = 4780
				}
			}
			cede_province = MAC
			add_core = MAC
			remove_core = ROOT 
		}
		vassalize = MAC
		MAC = { set_capital = 3001 }
	}
	
	option = {
		name = cpbm_independence_europe.29.b
		every_owned_province = { 
			limit = {
				OR = { 
					province_id = 3001
					province_id = 4780
				}
			}
			cede_province = MAC
			add_core = MAC
			remove_core = ROOT 
		}
		MAC = { 
			every_neighbor_country = { add_truce_with = MAC } 
			set_capital = 3001
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = cpbm_independence_europe.29.c
		trigger = { AND = { adm_power = 100 dip_power = 100 mil_power = 100 } }
		add_adm_power = -200
		add_dip_power = -200
		add_mil_power = -200
		add_years_of_income = -2
		every_owned_province = { 
			limit = {
				OR = { 
					province_id = 3001
					province_id = 4780
				}
			}
			add_unrest = 5
			add_core = MAC
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = cpbm_independence_europe.29.dd
		every_owned_province = { 
			limit = {
				OR = { 
					province_id = 3001
					province_id = 4780
				}
			}
			cede_province = MAC
			add_core = MAC
		}
		MAC = { 
			declare_war_with_cb = {
				who = ROOT
				casus_belli = cb_independence_war
			}
			set_capital = 3001
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			MAC = {
				capital_scope = {
					build_to_forcelimit = {
						infantry = 0.8
						cavalry = 0.2
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}
    
    after = { 3001 = { every_core_country = { limit = { tag = MAC } change_primary_culture = PREV change_religion = PREV change_government = ROOT } }
		MAC = { every_province = { limit = { owned_by = ROOT is_in_capital_area = no NOT = { range = ROOT } trade_range = PREV } cede_province = PREV add_core = PREV }
		every_owned_province = { limit = { is_in_capital_area = no NOT = { range = PREV } trade_range = ROOT } cede_province = ROOT add_core = ROOT } }
		random_list = { 1 = { country_event = { id = cpbm_independence_trigger.1 } } 9 = { } }
	}
}

					province_id = 38
					province_id = 39
					province_id = 273
					province_id = 1935
					province_id = 4241
				}
			}
			cede_province = LTV
			add_core = LTV
		}
		LTV = { 
			declare_war_with_cb = {
				who = ROOT
				casus_belli = cb_independence_war
			}
			set_capital = 38
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			LTV = {
				capital_scope = {
					build_to_forcelimit = {
						infantry = 0.8
						cavalry = 0.2
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}
    
    after = { 38 = { every_core_country = { limit = { tag = LTV } change_primary_culture = PREV change_religion = PREV change_government = ROOT } }
		LTV = { every_province = { limit = { owned_by = ROOT is_in_capital_area = no NOT = { range = ROOT } trade_range = PREV } cede_province = PREV add_core = PREV }
		every_owned_province = { limit = { is_in_capital_area = no NOT = { range = PREV } trade_range = ROOT } cede_province = ROOT add_core = ROOT } }
		random_list = { 1 = { country_event = { id = cpbm_independence_trigger.1 } } 9 = { } }
	}
}

#Lithuania
country_event = {
	id = cpbm_independence_europe.36
	title = cpbm_independence_europe.36.t
	desc = cpbm_independence_europe.36.d
	picture = MILITARY_CAMP_eventPicture

	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	option = {
		name = cpbm_independence_europe.36.a
		add_adm_power = -200
		add_dip_power = -200
		add_mil_power = -200
		every_owned_province = { 
			limit = {
				OR = { 
                    area = lithuania_area
                    area = samogitia_area
					province_id = 40
				}
			}
			cede_province = LIT
			add_core = LIT
			remove_core = ROOT 
		}
		vassalize = LIT
		LIT = { set_capital = 272 }
	}
	
	option = {
		name = cpbm_independence_europe.36.b
		every_owned_province = { 
			limit = {
				OR = { 
                    area = lithuania_area
                    area = samogitia_area
					province_id = 40
				}
			}
			cede_province = LIT
			add_core = LIT
			remove_core = ROOT 
		}
		LIT = { 
			every_neighbor_country = { add_truce_with = LIT } 
			set_capital = 272
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = cpbm_independence_europe.36.c
		trigger = { AND = { adm_power = 100 dip_power = 100 mil_power = 100 } }
		add_adm_power = -200
		add_dip_power = -200
		add_mil_power = -200
		add_years_of_income = -2
		every_owned_province = { 
			limit = {
				OR = { 
                    area = lithuania_area
                    area = samogitia_area
					province_id = 40
				}
			}
			add_unrest = 5
			add_core = LIT
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = cpbm_independence_europe.36.dd
		every_owned_province = { 
			limit = {
				OR = { 
                    area = lithuania_area
                    area = samogitia_area
					province_id = 40
				}
			}
			cede_province = LIT
			add_core = LIT
		}
		LIT = { 
			declare_war_with_cb = {
				who = ROOT
				casus_belli = cb_independence_war
			}
			set_capital = 272
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			LIT = {
				capital_scope = {
					build_to_forcelimit = {
						infantry = 0.8
						cavalry = 0.2
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}
    
    after = { 272 = { every_core_country = { limit = { tag = LIT } change_primary_culture = PREV change_religion = PREV change_government = ROOT } }
		LIT = { every_province = { limit = { owned_by = ROOT is_in_capital_area = no NOT = { range = ROOT } trade_range = PREV } cede_province = PREV add_core = PREV }
		every_owned_province = { limit = { is_in_capital_area = no NOT = { range = PREV } trade_range = ROOT } cede_province = ROOT add_core = ROOT } }
		random_list = { 1 = { country_event = { id = cpbm_independence_trigger.1 } } 9 = { } }

country_event = {
	id = cpbm_independence_europe.43
	title = cpbm_independence_europe.43.t
	desc = cpbm_independence_europe.43.d
	picture = MILITARY_CAMP_eventPicture

	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	option = {
		name = cpbm_independence_europe.43.a
		add_adm_power = -200
		add_dip_power = -200
		add_mil_power = -200
		every_owned_province = { 
			limit = {
				OR = { 
                    area = laponia_area
					province_id = 18
					province_id = 4114
					province_id = 4151
				}
			}
			cede_province = SMI
			add_core = SMI
			remove_core = ROOT 
		}
		vassalize = SMI
		SMI = { set_capital = 4152 }
	}
	
	option = {
		name = cpbm_independence_europe.43.b
		every_owned_province = { 
			limit = {
				OR = { 
                    area = laponia_area
					province_id = 18
					province_id = 4114
					province_id = 4151
				}
			}
			cede_province = SMI
			add_core = SMI
			remove_core = ROOT 
		}
		SMI = { 
			every_neighbor_country = { add_truce_with = SMI } 
			set_capital = 4152
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = cpbm_independence_europe.43.c
		trigger = { AND = { adm_power = 100 dip_power = 100 mil_power = 100 } }
		add_adm_power = -200
		add_dip_power = -200
		add_mil_power = -200
		add_years_of_income = -2
		every_owned_province = { 
			limit = {
				OR = { 
                    area = laponia_area
					province_id = 18
					province_id = 4114
					province_id = 4151
				}
			}
			add_unrest = 5
			add_core = SMI
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = cpbm_independence_europe.43.dd
		every_owned_province = { 
			limit = {
				OR = { 
                    area = laponia_area
					province_id = 18
					province_id = 4114
					province_id = 4151
				}
			}
			cede_province = SMI
			add_core = SMI
		}
		SMI = { 
			declare_war_with_cb = {
				who = ROOT
				casus_belli = cb_independence_war
			}
			set_capital = 4152
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			SMI = {
				capital_scope = {
					build_to_forcelimit = {
						infantry = 0.8
						cavalry = 0.2
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}
    
    after = { 4152 = { every_core_country = { limit = { tag = SMI } change_primary_culture = PREV change_religion = PREV change_government = ROOT } }
		SMI = { every_province = { limit = { owned_by = ROOT is_in_capital_area = no NOT = { range = ROOT } trade_range = PREV } cede_province = PREV add_core = PREV }
		every_owned_province = { limit = { is_in_capital_area = no NOT = { range = PREV } trade_range = ROOT } cede_province = ROOT add_core = ROOT } }

		name = cpbm_independence_europe.56.b
		every_owned_province = { 
			limit = {
				OR = { 
                    area = lazio_area
					province_id = 113
					province_id = 114
					province_id = 119
					province_id = 1247
					province_id = 2977
					province_id = 4730
				}
			}
			cede_province = PAP
			add_core = PAP
			remove_core = ROOT 
		}
		PAP = { 
			every_neighbor_country = { add_truce_with = PAP } 
			set_capital = 118
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = cpbm_independence_europe.56.c
		trigger = { AND = { adm_power = 100 dip_power = 100 mil_power = 100 } }
		add_adm_power = -200
		add_dip_power = -200
		add_mil_power = -200
		add_years_of_income = -2

			limit = {
				OR = { 
                    area = lazio_area
					province_id = 113
					province_id = 114
					province_id = 119
					province_id = 1247
					province_id = 2977
					province_id = 4730
				}
			}
			add_unrest = 5
			add_core = PAP
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = cpbm_independence_europe.56.dd
		every_owned_province = { 
			limit = {
				OR = { 
                    area = lazio_area
					province_id = 113
					province_id = 114

					province_id = 2977
					province_id = 4730
				}
			}
			cede_province = PAP
			add_core = PAP
		}
		PAP = { 
			declare_war_with_cb = {
				who = ROOT
				casus_belli = cb_independence_war
			}
			set_capital = 118
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			PAP = {
				capital_scope = {
					build_to_forcelimit = {
						infantry = 0.8
						cavalry = 0.2
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}
    
    after = { 118 = { every_core_country = { limit = { tag = PAP } change_primary_culture = PREV change_religion = PREV change_government = ROOT } }
		PAP = { every_province = { limit = { owned_by = ROOT is_in_capital_area = no NOT = { range = ROOT } trade_range = PREV } cede_province = PREV add_core = PREV }

		name = cpbm_independence_europe.58.a

		add_dip_power = -200
		add_mil_power = -200
		every_owned_province = { 
			limit = {
				OR = { 
                    area = ile_de_france_area
                    area = normandy_area
                    area = champagne_area

                    area = picardy_area
                    area = west_burgundy_area
                    area = loire_area
                    area = poitou_area
                    area = guyenne_area
                    area = languedoc_area
                    area = pyrenees_area
					province_id = 172
					province_id = 190
					province_id = 192
					province_id = 195
					province_id = 199
					province_id = 4697
					province_id = 4769
				}
			}
			cede_province = FRW
			add_core = FRW
			remove_core = ROOT 
		}

	}

                    area = west_burgundy_area
                    area = loire_area
                    area = poitou_area
                    area = guyenne_area
                    area = languedoc_area
                    area = pyrenees_area
					province_id = 172

					province_id = 195

					province_id = 4697
					province_id = 4769

			add_unrest = 5

	option = {

                    area = ile_de_france_area

					}
				}
			}
		}
	}
    
    after = { 
		183 = { every_core_country = { limit = { tag = FRW } change_primary_culture = PREV change_religion = PREV change_government = monarchy } }
		FRW = { 
			set_dynasty = "Carolingian"
            every_province = { limit = { owned_by = ROOT is_in_capital_area = no NOT = { range = ROOT } trade_range = PREV } cede_province = PREV add_core = PREV }

    }

		add_adm_power = -200
		add_dip_power = -200
		add_mil_power = -200
		add_years_of_income = -2
		every_owned_province = { 
			limit = {
				OR = { 
                    area = valencia_area
					province_id = 221
				}
			}
			add_unrest = 5
			add_core = VAL
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = cpbm_independence_europe.69.dd
		every_owned_province = { 
			limit = {
				OR = { 
                    area = valencia_area
					province_id = 221
				}
			}
			cede_province = VAL
			add_core = VAL
		}
		VAL = { 
			declare_war_with_cb = {
				who = ROOT
				casus_belli = cb_independence_war
			}
			set_capital = 220
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			VAL = {
				capital_scope = {
					build_to_forcelimit = {
						infantry = 0.8
						cavalry = 0.2
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}
    
    after = { 220 = { every_core_country = { limit = { tag = VAL } change_primary_culture = PREV change_religion = PREV change_government = ROOT } }
		VAL = { every_province = { limit = { owned_by = ROOT is_in_capital_area = no NOT = { range = ROOT } trade_range = PREV } cede_province = PREV add_core = PREV }
		every_owned_province = { limit = { is_in_capital_area = no NOT = { range = PREV } trade_range = ROOT } cede_province = ROOT add_core = ROOT } }

			remove_core = ROOT 
		}
		vassalize = AUV
		AUV = { set_capital = 199 }
	}
	
	option = {
		name = cpbm_independence_europe.77.b
		every_owned_province = { 
			limit = {
				OR = { 
					province_id = 190
					province_id = 198
					province_id = 199
				}
			}
			cede_province = AUV
			add_core = AUV
			remove_core = ROOT 
		}
		AUV = { 
			every_neighbor_country = { add_truce_with = AUV } 
			set_capital = 199
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = cpbm_independence_europe.77.c
		trigger = { AND = { adm_power = 100 dip_power = 100 mil_power = 100 } }
		add_adm_power = -200
		add_dip_power = -200
		add_mil_power = -200
		add_years_of_income = -2
		every_owned_province = { 
			limit = {
				OR = { 
					province_id = 190
					province_id = 198
					province_id = 199
				}
			}
			add_unrest = 5
			add_core = AUV
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = cpbm_independence_europe.77.dd
		every_owned_province = { 
			limit = {
				OR = { 
					province_id = 190
					province_id = 198
					province_id = 199
				}
			}
			cede_province = AUV
			add_core = AUV
		}
		AUV = { 
			declare_war_with_cb = {
				who = ROOT
				casus_belli = cb_independence_war
			}
			set_capital = 199
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			AUV = {
				capital_scope = {
					build_to_forcelimit = {
						infantry = 0.8
						cavalry = 0.2
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}
    
    after = { 199 = { every_core_country = { limit = { tag = AUV } change_primary_culture = PREV change_religion = PREV change_government = ROOT } }
		AUV = { every_province = { limit = { owned_by = ROOT is_in_capital_area = no NOT = { range = ROOT } trade_range = PREV } cede_province = PREV add_core = PREV }
		every_owned_province = { limit = { is_in_capital_area = no NOT = { range = PREV } trade_range = ROOT } cede_province = ROOT add_core = ROOT } }
		random_list = { 1 = { country_event = { id = cpbm_independence_trigger.1 } } 9 = { } }
	}
}

#Teutonic Order
country_event = {
	id = cpbm_independence_europe.78
	title = cpbm_independence_europe.78.t
	desc = cpbm_independence_europe.78.d
	picture = MILITARY_CAMP_eventPicture

	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	option = {
		name = cpbm_independence_europe.78.a
		add_adm_power = -200
		add_dip_power = -200
		add_mil_power = -200
		every_owned_province = { 
			limit = {
				OR = { 
                    area = west_prussia_area
                    area = east_prussia_area
					province_id = 271
				}
			}
			cede_province = TEU
			add_core = TEU
			remove_core = ROOT 
		}
		vassalize = TEU
		TEU = { set_capital = 1841 }
	}
	
	option = {
		name = cpbm_independence_europe.78.b

				OR = { 
                    area = west_prussia_area
                    area = east_prussia_area
					province_id = 271
				}

			remove_core = ROOT 
		}

		}
	}

		add_adm_power = -200
		add_dip_power = -200
		add_mil_power = -200

                    area = west_prussia_area
                    area = east_prussia_area
					province_id = 271
				}

			add_core = TEU

			}
			set_capital = 1841
		}

			TEU = {

					build_to_forcelimit = {
						infantry = 0.8
						cavalry = 0.2
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}
    
    after = { 1841 = { every_core_country = { limit = { tag = TEU } change_primary_culture = PREV change_religion = PREV change_government = ROOT } }
		TEU = { every_province = { limit = { owned_by = ROOT is_in_capital_area = no NOT = { range = ROOT } trade_range = PREV } cede_province = PREV add_core = PREV }
		every_owned_province = { limit = { is_in_capital_area = no NOT = { range = PREV } trade_range = ROOT } cede_province = ROOT add_core = ROOT } }

		name = cpbm_independence_europe.84.b
		every_owned_province = { 
			limit = { province_id = 272 }
			cede_province = VI3
			add_core = VI3
			remove_core = ROOT 
		}
		VI3 = { 
			every_neighbor_country = { add_truce_with = VI3 } 
			set_capital = 272
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = cpbm_independence_europe.84.c
		trigger = { AND = { adm_power = 100 dip_power = 100 mil_power = 100 } }
		add_adm_power = -200
		add_dip_power = -200
		add_mil_power = -200
		add_years_of_income = -2
		every_owned_province = { 
			limit = { province_id = 272 }
			add_unrest = 5
			add_core = VI3
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = cpbm_independence_europe.84.dd
		every_owned_province = { 
			limit = { province_id = 272 }
			cede_province = VI3
			add_core = VI3
		}
		VI3 = { 
			declare_war_with_cb = {
				who = ROOT
				casus_belli = cb_independence_war
			}
			set_capital = 272
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			VI3 = {
				capital_scope = {
					build_to_forcelimit = {
						infantry = 0.8
						cavalry = 0.2
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}
    
    after = { 272 = { every_core_country = { limit = { tag = VI3 } change_primary_culture = PREV change_religion = PREV change_government = ROOT } }
		VI3 = { every_province = { limit = { owned_by = ROOT is_in_capital_area = no NOT = { range = ROOT } trade_range = PREV } cede_province = PREV add_core = PREV }
		every_owned_province = { limit = { is_in_capital_area = no NOT = { range = PREV } trade_range = ROOT } cede_province = ROOT add_core = ROOT } }
		random_list = { 1 = { country_event = { id = cpbm_independence_trigger.1 } } 9 = { } }
	}
}

#Moravia
country_event = {
	id = cpbm_independence_europe.85
	title = cpbm_independence_europe.85.t
	desc = cpbm_independence_europe.85.d
	picture = MILITARY_CAMP_eventPicture

	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	option = {
		name = cpbm_independence_europe.85.a
		add_adm_power = -200
		add_dip_power = -200
		add_mil_power = -200
		every_owned_province = { 
			limit = {
				OR = { 
                    area = bohemia_area
                    area = erzgebirge_area
                    area = moravia_area
				}
			}
			cede_province = MVA
			add_core = MVA
			remove_core = ROOT 
		}
		vassalize = MVA
		MVA = { set_capital = 265 }
	}
	
	option = {
		name = cpbm_independence_europe.85.b
		every_owned_province = { 
			limit = {
				OR = { 
                    area = bohemia_area
                    area = erzgebirge_area
                    area = moravia_area
				}
			}
			cede_province = MVA
			add_core = MVA
			remove_core = ROOT 
		}

			every_neighbor_country = { add_truce_with = MVA } 
			set_capital = 265
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = cpbm_independence_europe.85.c
		trigger = { AND = { adm_power = 100 dip_power = 100 mil_power = 100 } }
		add_adm_power = -200
		add_dip_power = -200
		add_mil_power = -200

                    area = erzgebirge_area
                    area = moravia_area

                    area = erzgebirge_area

		}

					}
				}
			}
		}
	}
    
    after = { 265 = { every_core_country = { limit = { tag = MVA } change_primary_culture = PREV change_religion = PREV change_government = ROOT } }
		MVA = { every_province = { limit = { owned_by = ROOT is_in_capital_area = no NOT = { range = ROOT } trade_range = PREV } cede_province = PREV add_core = PREV }

country_event = {
	id = cpbm_independence_europe.87
	title = cpbm_independence_europe.87.t
	desc = cpbm_independence_europe.87.d
	picture = MILITARY_CAMP_eventPicture

	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	option = {
		name = cpbm_independence_europe.87.a
		add_adm_power = -200
		add_dip_power = -200
		add_mil_power = -200
		every_owned_province = { 
			limit = {
				OR = { 
                    area = north_rhine_area
                    area = lower_rhineland_area
                    area = westphalia_area
                    area = north_westphalia_area
                    area = hesse_area
                    area = braunschweig_area
                    area = weser_area
                    area = lower_saxony_area
                    area = franconia_area
                    area = palatinate_area
                    area = upper_franconia_area
                    area = lower_bavaria_area
                    area = upper_bavaria_area
                    area = upper_swabia_area
                    area = lower_swabia_area
                    area = upper_rhineland_area
					province_id = 13
					province_id = 45
					province_id = 1775
					province_id = 4141
					province_id = 4709
				}
			}
			cede_province = WGE
			add_core = WGE
			remove_core = ROOT 
		}
		vassalize = WGE
		WGE = { set_capital = 85 }
	}

                    area = hesse_area
                    area = braunschweig_area
                    area = weser_area
                    area = lower_saxony_area
                    area = franconia_area
                    area = palatinate_area
                    area = upper_franconia_area
                    area = lower_bavaria_area
                    area = upper_bavaria_area
                    area = upper_swabia_area

				capital_scope = {
					build_to_forcelimit = {
						infantry = 0.8
						cavalry = 0.2
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}
    
    after = { 85 = { every_core_country = { limit = { tag = KOL } change_primary_culture = PREV change_religion = PREV change_government = ROOT } }
		KOL = { every_province = { limit = { owned_by = ROOT is_in_capital_area = no NOT = { range = ROOT } trade_range = PREV } cede_province = PREV add_core = PREV }
		every_owned_province = { limit = { is_in_capital_area = no NOT = { range = PREV } trade_range = ROOT } cede_province = ROOT add_core = ROOT } }

#Visigoths
country_event = {
	id = cpbm_independence_europe.91
	title = cpbm_independence_europe.91.t
	desc = cpbm_independence_europe.91.d
	picture = MILITARY_CAMP_eventPicture

	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	option = {
		name = cpbm_independence_europe.91.a
		add_adm_power = -200
		add_dip_power = -200
		add_mil_power = -200
		every_owned_province = { 
			limit = {
				AND = { 
                    region = iberia_region
                    NOT = { area = baleares_area }
				}
			}
			cede_province = GVI
			add_core = GVI
			remove_core = ROOT 
		}
		vassalize = GVI
		GVI = { set_capital = 219 }
	}
	
	option = {
		name = cpbm_independence_europe.91.b
		every_owned_province = { 
			limit = {
				AND = { 
                    region = iberia_region
                    NOT = { area = baleares_area }
				}
			}
			cede_province = GVI
			add_core = GVI
			remove_core = ROOT 
		}
		GVI = { 
			every_neighbor_country = { add_truce_with = GVI } 
			set_capital = 219
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = cpbm_independence_europe.91.c
		trigger = { AND = { adm_power = 100 dip_power = 100 mil_power = 100 } }
		add_adm_power = -200
		add_dip_power = -200
		add_mil_power = -200
		add_years_of_income = -2
		every_owned_province = { 
			limit = {
				AND = { 
                    region = iberia_region
                    NOT = { area = baleares_area }
				}
			}
			add_unrest = 5
			add_core = GVI
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = cpbm_independence_europe.91.dd
		every_owned_province = { 
			limit = {
				AND = { 
                    region = iberia_region
                    NOT = { area = baleares_area }
				}
			}
			cede_province = GVI
			add_core = GVI
		}
		GVI = { 
			declare_war_with_cb = {
				who = ROOT
				casus_belli = cb_independence_war
			}
			set_capital = 219
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			GVI = {
				capital_scope = {
					build_to_forcelimit = {
						infantry = 0.8
						cavalry = 0.2
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}
    
    after = { 219 = { every_core_country = { limit = { tag = GVI } change_primary_culture = PREV change_religion = PREV change_government = ROOT } }
		GVI = { every_province = { limit = { owned_by = ROOT is_in_capital_area = no NOT = { range = ROOT } trade_range = PREV } cede_province = PREV add_core = PREV }
		every_owned_province = { limit = { is_in_capital_area = no NOT = { range = PREV } trade_range = ROOT } cede_province = ROOT add_core = ROOT } }
		random_list = { 1 = { country_event = { id = cpbm_independence_trigger.1 } } 9 = { } }
	}
}

#Frankfurt
country_event = {
	id = cpbm_independence_europe.99
	title = cpbm_independence_europe.99.t
	desc = cpbm_independence_europe.99.d
	picture = MILITARY_CAMP_eventPicture

	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	option = {
		name = cpbm_independence_europe.99.a
		add_adm_power = -200
		add_dip_power = -200
		add_mil_power = -200
		every_owned_province = { 
			limit = { province_id = 1876 }
			cede_province = FRN
			add_core = FRN
			remove_core = ROOT 
		}
		vassalize = FRN
		FRN = { set_capital = 1876 }
	}
	
	option = {
		name = cpbm_independence_europe.99.b
		every_owned_province = { 
			limit = { province_id = 1876 }
			cede_province = FRN
			add_core = FRN
			remove_core = ROOT 
		}
		FRN = { 
			every_neighbor_country = { add_truce_with = FRN } 
			set_capital = 1876
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = cpbm_independence_europe.99.c
		trigger = { AND = { adm_power = 100 dip_power = 100 mil_power = 100 } }
		add_adm_power = -200
		add_dip_power = -200
		add_mil_power = -200
		add_years_of_income = -2
		every_owned_province = { 
			limit = { province_id = 1876 }
			add_unrest = 5
			add_core = FRN
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = cpbm_independence_europe.99.dd
		every_owned_province = { 
			limit = { province_id = 1876 }
			cede_province = FRN
			add_core = FRN
		}
		FRN = { 
			declare_war_with_cb = {
				who = ROOT
				casus_belli = cb_independence_war
			}
			set_capital = 1876
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			FRN = {
				capital_scope = {
					build_to_forcelimit = {
						infantry = 0.8
						cavalry = 0.2
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}
    
    after = { 1876 = { every_core_country = { limit = { tag = FRN } change_primary_culture = PREV change_religion = PREV change_government = ROOT } }
		FRN = { every_province = { limit = { owned_by = ROOT is_in_capital_area = no NOT = { range = ROOT } trade_range = PREV } cede_province = PREV add_core = PREV }
		every_owned_province = { limit = { is_in_capital_area = no NOT = { range = PREV } trade_range = ROOT } cede_province = ROOT add_core = ROOT } }
		random_list = { 1 = { country_event = { id = cpbm_independence_trigger.1 } } 9 = { } }
	}
}

				}
			}
			cede_province = HES
			add_core = HES
			remove_core = ROOT 
		}
		HES = { 
			every_neighbor_country = { add_truce_with = HES } 
			set_capital = 81
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = cpbm_independence_europe.110.c
		trigger = { AND = { adm_power = 100 dip_power = 100 mil_power = 100 } }
		add_adm_power = -200
		add_dip_power = -200
		add_mil_power = -200
		add_years_of_income = -2
		every_owned_province = { 
			limit = {
				OR = { 
                    area = hesse_area
					province_id = 83
					province_id = 4718
				}
			}
			add_unrest = 5
			add_core = HES
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = cpbm_independence_europe.110.dd
		every_owned_province = { 
			limit = {
				OR = { 
                    area = hesse_area
					province_id = 83
					province_id = 4718
				}
			}
			cede_province = HES
			add_core = HES
		}
		HES = { 
			declare_war_with_cb = {
				who = ROOT
				casus_belli = cb_independence_war
			}
			set_capital = 81
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			HES = {
				capital_scope = {
					build_to_forcelimit = {
						infantry = 0.8
						cavalry = 0.2
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}
    
    after = { 81 = { every_core_country = { limit = { tag = HES } change_primary_culture = PREV change_religion = PREV change_government = ROOT } }
		HES = { every_province = { limit = { owned_by = ROOT is_in_capital_area = no NOT = { range = ROOT } trade_range = PREV } cede_province = PREV add_core = PREV }
		every_owned_province = { limit = { is_in_capital_area = no NOT = { range = PREV } trade_range = ROOT } cede_province = ROOT add_core = ROOT } }

#East Prussia
country_event = {
	id = cpbm_independence_europe.125
	title = cpbm_independence_europe.125.t
	desc = cpbm_independence_europe.125.d
	picture = MILITARY_CAMP_eventPicture

	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	option = {
		name = cpbm_independence_europe.125.a
		add_adm_power = -200
		add_dip_power = -200
		add_mil_power = -200
		every_owned_province = { 
			limit = {
				OR = { 
                    area = east_prussia_area
					province_id = 42
				}
			}
			cede_province = EP0
			add_core = EP0
			remove_core = ROOT 
		}
		vassalize = EP0
		EP0 = { set_capital = 41 }
	}
	
	option = {
		name = cpbm_independence_europe.125.b
		every_owned_province = { 
			limit = {
				OR = { 
                    area = east_prussia_area
					province_id = 42
				}
			}
			cede_province = EP0
			add_core = EP0
			remove_core = ROOT 
		}
		EP0 = { 
			every_neighbor_country = { add_truce_with = EP0 } 
			set_capital = 41
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = cpbm_independence_europe.125.c
		trigger = { AND = { adm_power = 100 dip_power = 100 mil_power = 100 } }
		add_adm_power = -200
		add_dip_power = -200
		add_mil_power = -200
		add_years_of_income = -2
		every_owned_province = { 
			limit = {
				OR = { 
                    area = east_prussia_area
					province_id = 42
				}
			}
			add_unrest = 5
			add_core = EP0
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = cpbm_independence_europe.125.dd
		every_owned_province = { 
			limit = {
				OR = { 
                    area = east_prussia_area
					province_id = 42
				}
			}
			cede_province = EP0
			add_core = EP0
		}
		EP0 = { 
			declare_war_with_cb = {
				who = ROOT
				casus_belli = cb_independence_war
			}
			set_capital = 41
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			EP0 = {
				capital_scope = {
					build_to_forcelimit = {
						infantry = 0.8
						cavalry = 0.2
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}
    
    after = { 41 = { every_core_country = { limit = { tag = EP0 } change_primary_culture = PREV change_religion = PREV change_government = ROOT } }
		EP0 = { every_province = { limit = { owned_by = ROOT is_in_capital_area = no NOT = { range = ROOT } trade_range = PREV } cede_province = PREV add_core = PREV }
		every_owned_province = { limit = { is_in_capital_area = no NOT = { range = PREV } trade_range = ROOT } cede_province = ROOT add_core = ROOT } }
		random_list = { 1 = { country_event = { id = cpbm_independence_trigger.1 } } 9 = { } }
	}
}

					province_id = 71
					province_id = 166
					province_id = 1869
					province_id = 1870
					province_id = 1872
					province_id = 4710
					province_id = 4715
				}
			}
			cede_province = SWA
			add_core = SWA
			remove_core = ROOT 
		}
		vassalize = SWA
		SWA = { set_capital = 70 }
	}
	
	option = {
		name = cpbm_independence_europe.132.b
		every_owned_province = { 
			limit = {
				OR = { 
                    area = lower_swabia_area
                    area = upper_rhineland_area
                    area = alsace_area
					province_id = 68
					province_id = 71
					province_id = 166
					province_id = 1869
					province_id = 1870
					province_id = 1872
					province_id = 4710
					province_id = 4715
				}
			}
			cede_province = SWA
			add_core = SWA
			remove_core = ROOT 
		}
		SWA = { 
			every_neighbor_country = { add_truce_with = SWA } 
			set_capital = 70
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = cpbm_independence_europe.132.c
		trigger = { AND = { adm_power = 100 dip_power = 100 mil_power = 100 } }
		add_adm_power = -200
		add_dip_power = -200
		add_mil_power = -200
		add_years_of_income = -2
		every_owned_province = { 
			limit = {
				OR = { 
                    area = lower_swabia_area
                    area = upper_rhineland_area
                    area = alsace_area
					province_id = 68
					province_id = 71
					province_id = 166
					province_id = 1869
					province_id = 1870
					province_id = 1872
					province_id = 4710
					province_id = 4715
				}
			}
			add_unrest = 5
			add_core = SWA
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = cpbm_independence_europe.132.dd
		every_owned_province = { 
			limit = {
				OR = { 
                    area = lower_swabia_area
                    area = upper_rhineland_area
                    area = alsace_area
					province_id = 68
					province_id = 71
					province_id = 166
					province_id = 1869
					province_id = 1870
					province_id = 1872
					province_id = 4710
					province_id = 4715
				}
			}
			cede_province = SWA
			add_core = SWA
		}
		SWA = { 
			declare_war_with_cb = {
				who = ROOT
				casus_belli = cb_independence_war
			}
			set_capital = 70
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			SWA = {
				capital_scope = {
					build_to_forcelimit = {
						infantry = 0.8
						cavalry = 0.2
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}
    
    after = { 70 = { every_core_country = { limit = { tag = SWA } change_primary_culture = PREV change_religion = PREV change_government = ROOT } }
		SWA = { every_province = { limit = { owned_by = ROOT is_in_capital_area = no NOT = { range = ROOT } trade_range = PREV } cede_province = PREV add_core = PREV }
		every_owned_province = { limit = { is_in_capital_area = no NOT = { range = PREV } trade_range = ROOT } cede_province = ROOT add_core = ROOT } }

#Vestlandet
country_event = {
	id = cpbm_independence_europe.140
	title = cpbm_independence_europe.140.t
	desc = cpbm_independence_europe.140.d
	picture = MILITARY_CAMP_eventPicture

	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	option = {
		name = cpbm_independence_europe.140.a
		add_adm_power = -200
		add_dip_power = -200
		add_mil_power = -200
		every_owned_province = { 
			limit = {
				OR = { 
					province_id = 23
					province_id = 24
					province_id = 2752
				}
			}
			cede_province = VS1
			add_core = VS1
			remove_core = ROOT 
		}
		vassalize = VS1
		VS1 = { set_capital = 23 }
	}
	
	option = {
		name = cpbm_independence_europe.140.b
		every_owned_province = { 
			limit = {
				OR = { 
					province_id = 23
					province_id = 24
					province_id = 2752
				}
			}
			cede_province = VS1
			add_core = VS1
			remove_core = ROOT 
		}
		VS1 = { 
			every_neighbor_country = { add_truce_with = VS1 } 
			set_capital = 23
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = cpbm_independence_europe.140.c
		trigger = { AND = { adm_power = 100 dip_power = 100 mil_power = 100 } }
		add_adm_power = -200
		add_dip_power = -200
		add_mil_power = -200
		add_years_of_income = -2
		every_owned_province = { 
			limit = {
				OR = { 
					province_id = 23
					province_id = 24
					province_id = 2752
				}
			}
			add_unrest = 5
			add_core = VS1
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = cpbm_independence_europe.140.dd
		every_owned_province = { 
			limit = {
				OR = { 
					province_id = 23
					province_id = 24
					province_id = 2752
				}
			}
			cede_province = VS1
			add_core = VS1
		}
		VS1 = { 
			declare_war_with_cb = {
				who = ROOT
				casus_belli = cb_independence_war
			}
			set_capital = 23
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			VS1 = {
				capital_scope = {
					build_to_forcelimit = {
						infantry = 0.8
						cavalry = 0.2
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}
    
    after = { 23 = { every_core_country = { limit = { tag = VS1 } change_primary_culture = PREV change_religion = PREV change_government = ROOT } }
		VS1 = { every_province = { limit = { owned_by = ROOT is_in_capital_area = no NOT = { range = ROOT } trade_range = PREV } cede_province = PREV add_core = PREV }
		every_owned_province = { limit = { is_in_capital_area = no NOT = { range = PREV } trade_range = ROOT } cede_province = ROOT add_core = ROOT } }
		random_list = { 1 = { country_event = { id = cpbm_independence_trigger.1 } } 9 = { } }
	}
}

					province_id = 1777
					province_id = 4113
					province_id = 4152
				}
			}
			cede_province = KO2
			add_core = KO2
			remove_core = ROOT 
		}
		KO2 = { 
			every_neighbor_country = { add_truce_with = KO2 } 
			set_capital = 4113
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = cpbm_independence_europe.147.c
		trigger = { AND = { adm_power = 100 dip_power = 100 mil_power = 100 } }
		add_adm_power = -200
		add_dip_power = -200
		add_mil_power = -200
		add_years_of_income = -2
		every_owned_province = { 
			limit = {
				OR = { 
					province_id = 1777
					province_id = 4113
					province_id = 4152
				}
			}
			add_unrest = 5
			add_core = KO2
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = cpbm_independence_europe.147.dd
		every_owned_province = { 
			limit = {
				OR = { 
					province_id = 1777
					province_id = 4113
					province_id = 4152
				}
			}
			cede_province = KO2
			add_core = KO2
		}
		KO2 = { 
			declare_war_with_cb = {
				who = ROOT
				casus_belli = cb_independence_war
			}
			set_capital = 4113
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			KO2 = {
				capital_scope = {
					build_to_forcelimit = {
						infantry = 0.8
						cavalry = 0.2
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}
    
    after = { 4113 = { every_core_country = { limit = { tag = KO2 } change_primary_culture = PREV change_religion = PREV change_government = ROOT } }
		KO2 = { every_province = { limit = { owned_by = ROOT is_in_capital_area = no NOT = { range = ROOT } trade_range = PREV } cede_province = PREV add_core = PREV }
		every_owned_province = { limit = { is_in_capital_area = no NOT = { range = PREV } trade_range = ROOT } cede_province = ROOT add_core = ROOT } }
		random_list = { 1 = { country_event = { id = cpbm_independence_trigger.1 } } 9 = { } }
	}
